81	An emergency ordinance |184	authorizing the Director of Public Service to issue a permit to The Nottingham Civic
73	Club to encroach into various locations of the public right-of-way in the areas of St. Clair Avenue and Notting-
73	ham Road, with a total of both (approximately) thirty-one (31) banners and American flags to publicize the “Not-
